           <h1 name="e616" id="e616" class="graf graf--h3 graf--leading graf--title">Start a Premium Content Business Using Node.js, React and Cosmic JS Extensions</h1>
          </div>
          <div class="section-inner sectionLayout--outsetColumn">
           <figure name="c001" id="c001" class="graf graf--figure graf--layoutOutsetCenter graf-after--h3">
            <div class="aspectRatioPlaceholder is-locked" style="max-width: 1000px; max-height: 670px;">
             <div class="aspectRatioPlaceholder-fill" style="padding-bottom: 67%;"></div>
             <div class="progressiveMedia js-progressiveMedia graf-image" data-image-id="1*_aAbFp-zaWY0gcVkBLul1g.jpeg" data-width="2987" data-height="2000" data-action="zoom" data-action-value="1*_aAbFp-zaWY0gcVkBLul1g.jpeg">
              <img src="https://cdn-images-1.medium.com/freeze/max/60/1*_aAbFp-zaWY0gcVkBLul1g.jpeg?q=20" crossorigin="anonymous" class="progressiveMedia-thumbnail js-progressiveMedia-thumbnail">
              <canvas class="progressiveMedia-canvas js-progressiveMedia-canvas"></canvas>
              <img class="progressiveMedia-image js-progressiveMedia-image" data-src="https://cdn-images-1.medium.com/max/2000/1*_aAbFp-zaWY0gcVkBLul1g.jpeg">
              <noscript class="js-progressiveMedia-inner">
               <img class="progressiveMedia-noscript js-progressiveMedia-inner" src="https://cdn-images-1.medium.com/max/2000/1*_aAbFp-zaWY0gcVkBLul1g.jpeg">
              </noscript>
             </div>
            </div>
           </figure>
          </div>
          <div class="section-inner sectionLayout--insetColumn">
           <h3 name="a196" id="a196" class="graf graf--h3 graf-after--figure">TL;DR</h3>
           <p name="2e03" id="2e03" class="graf graf--p graf-after--h3"><a href="https://cosmicjs.com/apps/premium-content-blog/demo" data-href="https://cosmicjs.com/apps/premium-content-blog/demo" class="markup--anchor markup--p-anchor" rel="noopener noreferrer noopener" target="_blank">View the demo</a><br><a href="https://github.com/cosmicjs/premium-content-blog" data-href="https://github.com/cosmicjs/premium-content-blog" class="markup--anchor markup--p-anchor" rel="noopener noreferrer noopener" target="_blank">View the source code</a><br><a href="https://cosmicjs.com/apps/premium-content-blog" data-href="https://cosmicjs.com/apps/premium-content-blog" class="markup--anchor markup--p-anchor" rel="noopener" target="_blank">Install the Premium Content Blog</a></p>
           <p name="1927" id="1927" class="graf graf--p graf-after--p">You have great ideas. Your head is overflowing with content that you <em class="markup--em markup--p-em">know</em> people will pay to read. So where do you start? You’re likely inclined to choose a trusted platform like Wordpress, but since you want to offer paid content to your users you now face the problem of making a cumbersome solution even more so.</p>
           <p name="ed4c" id="ed4c" class="graf graf--p graf-after--p">Instead of tweaking a platform to work with for us, we want a simple, straightforward solution with no more functionality than we need. This, of course, means we’re going to build it ourselves.</p>
           <p name="6c1f" id="6c1f" class="graf graf--p graf-after--p">In the spirit of a simple, straight forward solution that works exactly the way we want it to, we’ll be using <a href="https://cosmicjs.com" data-href="https://cosmicjs.com" class="markup--anchor markup--p-anchor" rel="noopener" target="_blank">Cosmic JS</a> to host our blog, manage it’s users, and store it’s content.</p>
           <p name="00f2" id="00f2" class="graf graf--p graf-after--p">Our project will be a play in two parts. First, we’ll build our blog with Express and Cosmic JS and use Stripe to handle the blog’s payments and subcriptions. Then, we’ll leverage Cosmic JS’s Extension feature to build a dashboard that gives us an overview of our business’ backend.</p>
           <h3 name="9af9" id="9af9" class="graf graf--h3 graf-after--p">Part 1: Building the&nbsp;Blog</h3>
           <h3 name="6b72" id="6b72" class="graf graf--h3 graf-after--h3">1. Boilerplate Setup</h3>
           <p name="1486" id="1486" class="graf graf--p graf-after--h3">To save time on boilerplate, we’ll use Yeoman and the Express Generator (which builds on Express’ official generator) to get started. If you don’t have Yeoman installed, run <code class="markup--code markup--p-code">npm i -g yo</code>. Then install the generator with <code class="markup--code markup--p-code">npm i -g generator-express</code> and run it with <code class="markup--code markup--p-code">yo express</code>. Follow the instructions to set up your project under a new directory (say <code class="markup--code markup--p-code">CosmicUserBlog</code>), install the <em class="markup--em markup--p-em">Basic</em> version, and use Handlebars for your view engine.</p>
           <p name="4a53" id="4a53" class="graf graf--p graf-after--p">Your directory structure is now this:</p>
           <pre name="3484" id="3484" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--p">CosmicUserBlog<br>| <br>|--bin<br>|   |--www<br>|--(node_modules)<br>|--public<br>|--routes<br>|    |--users.js<br>     |--index.js<br>|--views<br>     |--layouts<br>     |--partials<br>     |--error.handlebars<br>     |--index.handlebars<br>|--.bowerrc<br>|--.gitignore<br>|--app.js<br>|--bower.json<br>|--gruntfile.js<br>|--package.json</pre>
           <h3 name="2cec" id="2cec" class="graf graf--h3 graf-after--pre">2. Installations</h3>
           <p name="fc3d" id="fc3d" class="graf graf--p graf-after--h3">We’ll be using the following packages:</p>
           <ul class="postList">
            <li name="92bb" id="92bb" class="graf graf--li graf-after--p">Async?—?A powerful async utilities library</li>
            <li name="8860" id="8860" class="graf graf--li graf-after--li">Axios?—?Simple, promise based http requests</li>
            <li name="789d" id="789d" class="graf graf--li graf-after--li">Cors?—?Standard cors middleware</li>
            <li name="203f" id="203f" class="graf graf--li graf-after--li">brcypt?—?For password hashing. (If you’re on Windows read <a href="https://www.npmjs.com/package/bcrypt#dependencies" data-href="https://www.npmjs.com/package/bcrypt#dependencies" class="markup--anchor markup--li-anchor" rel="noopener" target="_blank">these notes</a>)</li>
            <li name="484b" id="484b" class="graf graf--li graf-after--li">CosmicJs?—?The official client</li>
            <li name="a96b" id="a96b" class="graf graf--li graf-after--li">Express Session?—?So our users can log in</li>
            <li name="16f8" id="16f8" class="graf graf--li graf-after--li">dateformat?—?An intuitive date formatter that we’ll use with posts</li>
            <li name="2a01" id="2a01" class="graf graf--li graf-after--li">Stripe?—?The official client</li>
            <li name="39f1" id="39f1" class="graf graf--li graf-after--li">TruncateHTML?—?for post blurbs</li>
           </ul>
           <p name="0c8f" id="0c8f" class="graf graf--p graf-after--li">You could install these with npm, but I advocate for Yarn. It’s significantly faster and we have no time to waste. So install Yarn (on macOS we’ll do a <code class="markup--code markup--p-code">brew install yarn</code>) then run <code class="markup--code markup--p-code">yarn add async axios cors bcrypt cosmicjs expres-session dateformat stripe truncate-html</code>&nbsp;. We're almost ready to start building.</p>
           <h3 name="f8c9" id="f8c9" class="graf graf--h3 graf-after--p">3. Set Up Cosmic&nbsp;JS</h3>
           <p name="7eef" id="7eef" class="graf graf--p graf-after--h3">Before we start building, we’ll need to work out the schema for our Cosmic Bucket. We want to store <code class="markup--code markup--p-code">Posts</code>, <code class="markup--code markup--p-code">Users</code>, and <code class="markup--code markup--p-code">Configs</code> (to edit site configurations on the fly).</p>
           <p name="3559" id="3559" class="graf graf--p graf-after--p">Those three object types will have the following matafields (all of type <em class="markup--em markup--p-em">text</em>, given by their <em class="markup--em markup--p-em">Title</em>):</p>
           <h4 name="37e4" id="37e4" class="graf graf--h4 graf-after--p">Post:</h4>
           <p name="f108" id="f108" class="graf graf--p graf-after--h4">MetafieldValuePremium<strong class="markup--strong markup--p-strong">true</strong> or <strong class="markup--strong markup--p-strong">false</strong></p>
           <h4 name="83fe" id="83fe" class="graf graf--h4 graf-after--p">User:</h4>
           <p name="d1de" id="d1de" class="graf graf--p graf-after--h4">MetafieldValueFirst namestringLast namestringPasswordHashed StringEmailstringStripe IdstringSubsription Typestring</p>
           <h4 name="7802" id="7802" class="graf graf--h4 graf-after--p">Config:</h4>
           <p name="3263" id="3263" class="graf graf--p graf-after--h4"><strong class="markup--strong markup--p-strong">Object: Subscriptions</strong>: | Metafield | Value | |?—?—?—?—?—?—?—?— |?—?— -: | | Monthly Price | string | | Quarterly Price | string | | Yearly Price | string | | Cancellations | string |</p>
           <p name="843d" id="843d" class="graf graf--p graf-after--p"><strong class="markup--strong markup--p-strong">Object: Site</strong>: | Metafield | Value | |?—?—?—?—?—?|?—?— -: | | Site Title | string | | Domain | String |</p>
           <p name="200c" id="200c" class="graf graf--p graf-after--p">Once you’ve added your <code class="markup--code markup--p-code">Post</code>, <code class="markup--code markup--p-code">User</code>, and <code class="markup--code markup--p-code">Config</code> object types and created your <code class="markup--code markup--p-code">Subscriptions</code> and <code class="markup--code markup--p-code">Site</code> Config objects, we'll get ourselves set up with Stripe.</p>
           <h3 name="ebce" id="ebce" class="graf graf--h3 graf-after--p">4. Configure Stripe</h3>
           <p name="cdf4" id="cdf4" class="graf graf--p graf-after--h3">Since we’ll be charging users for their premium subscriptions we’ll need a payment processor. With a robust API, fair pay-as-you-go pricing, and proven security, using Stripe is a no brainer. Moving foward, we’ll need both a “Publishable” and a “Secret” key for Stripe’s API and we need to setup Subscription plans for Monthly, Yearly, and Quarterly subscriptions. Follow Stripe’s instructions to create these subscriptions and give them the ID’s <em class="markup--em markup--p-em">subscription-monthly</em>, <em class="markup--em markup--p-em">subscription-quarterly</em>, and <em class="markup--em markup--p-em">subscription-yearly</em> accordingly.</p>
           <h3 name="b80b" id="b80b" class="graf graf--h3 graf-after--p">5. Configure the Express&nbsp;App</h3>
           <p name="c134" id="c134" class="graf graf--p graf-after--h3">We have our packages installed, we worked out our data schema, and we’ve set up a a Stripe account. Now we need to configure our Express backend.</p>
           <p name="35ee" id="35ee" class="graf graf--p graf-after--p">The boilerplate Express code is pre-ES5, so for a consistent style we’ll <code class="markup--code markup--p-code">require</code> the packages we need.</p>
           <p name="921c" id="921c" class="graf graf--p graf-after--p">At the top of the Express app add:</p>
           <pre name="d3a6" id="d3a6" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--p">// app.js<br>var session = require('express-session')<br>var dateFormat = require('date-format')<br>var truncate = require('truncate-html')<br>var cors = require('cors')</pre>
           <p name="a661" id="a661" class="graf graf--p graf-after--pre">When we deploy our app, Cosmic JS will provide our Bucket keys as well as any custom keys we provide via <code class="markup--code markup--p-code">process.env</code>. Below the require statements, go ahead make those accessible throughout the app by storing them in <code class="markup--code markup--p-code">app.locals</code></p>
           <pre name="9493" id="9493" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--p">//app.js</pre>
           <pre name="fca6" id="fca6" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--pre">var config = {<br>    bucket: {<br>        slug: process.env.COSMIC_BUCKET,<br>     read_key: process.env.COSMIC_READ_KEY,<br>      write_key: process.env.COSMIC_WRITE_KEY<br>    }<br>}<br>app.locals.config = config<br>app.locals.stripeKeyPublishable = process.env.STRIPE_PUBLISHABLE_KEY<br>app.locals.stripeKeySecret = process.env.STRIPE_SECRET_KEY</pre>
           <p name="bdc9" id="bdc9" class="graf graf--p graf-after--pre">The last step is then to connect the <code class="markup--code markup--p-code">cors</code> and <code class="markup--code markup--p-code">session</code> middleware like so:</p>
           <pre name="10a6" id="10a6" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--p">//app.js</pre>
           <pre name="d988" id="d988" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--pre">app.locals.stripeKeySecret = process.env.STRIPE_SECRET_KEY</pre>
           <pre name="ad36" id="ad36" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--pre">app.use(session({<br>  secret: 'sjcimsoc',<br>  resave: false,<br>  saveUninitialized: true,<br>  cookie: { secure: false }<br>}))<br>app.use(cors())</pre>
           <p name="3ecc" id="3ecc" class="graf graf--p graf-after--pre">At this point we have a solid base to build our app on and can start drafting out it’s views.</p>
           <h3 name="0d4d" id="0d4d" class="graf graf--h3 graf-after--p">6. Sculpt Out the&nbsp;Views</h3>
           <p name="d0cd" id="d0cd" class="graf graf--p graf-after--h3">Having a model of how we want our blog to look and feel will help us think about how to wire up it’s routes. We’ll start with the main layout.</p>
           <p name="e5c4" id="e5c4" class="graf graf--p graf-after--p"><strong class="markup--strong markup--p-strong">The Main Layout:</strong></p>
           <p name="b8f5" id="b8f5" class="graf graf--p graf-after--p">In handlebars, every page will render inside the <code class="markup--code markup--p-code">body</code> tag of a default layout. In our boilerplate, this is <code class="markup--code markup--p-code">/views/layouts/main.handlebars</code>.</p>
           <p name="e259" id="e259" class="graf graf--p graf-after--p">We need to make three alterations.</p>
           <ol class="postList">
            <li name="1636" id="1636" class="graf graf--li graf-after--p">in the <code class="markup--code markup--li-code">title</code> tag, swap out <code class="markup--code markup--li-code">{{title}}</code> for <code class="markup--code markup--li-code">{{config.site_title}}</code>, which we'll pass via <code class="markup--code markup--li-code">res.locals</code> later.</li>
            <li name="71f8" id="71f8" class="graf graf--li graf-after--li">Before the end of the <code class="markup--code markup--li-code">head</code> tag add <code class="markup--code markup--li-code">&lt;script src="https://js.stripe.com/v3/"&gt;&lt;/script&gt;</code>. This is Stripe's browser client. We only need this for the checkout form, however Stripe reccomends including it on every page to aid in fraud detection.</li>
            <li name="f320" id="f320" class="graf graf--li graf-after--li">Include Bootstrap. Somewhere in the <code class="markup--code markup--li-code">head</code> tag add <code class="markup--code markup--li-code">&lt;link rel="stylesheet" href="https://maxcdn.bootstrapcdn.com/bootstrap/3.3.7/css/bootstrap.min.css" /&gt;</code> and right before the end of the <code class="markup--code markup--li-code">body</code> tag add</li>
           </ol>
           <pre name="b84e" id="b84e" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--li"><code class="markup--code markup--pre-code">&lt;script src="https://code.jquery.com/jquery-3.2.1.min.js"<br> integrity="sha256-hwg4gsxgFZhOsEEamdOYGBf13FyQuiTwlAQgxVSNgt4="<br> crossorigin="anonymous"&gt;&lt;/script&gt;<br>&lt;script src="https://maxcdn.bootstrapcdn.com/bootstrap/3.3.7/js/bootstrap.min.js"&gt;&lt;/script&gt;</code></pre>
           <p name="b88b" id="b88b" class="graf graf--p graf-after--pre">The Main layout now looks like this:</p>
           <pre name="3139" id="3139" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--p">&lt;!-- views/layouts/main.handlebars --&gt;<br>&lt;!doctype html&gt;<br>&lt;html lang="en"&gt;<br>  &lt;head&gt;<br>    &lt;meta charset="UTF-8"&gt;<br>    &lt;meta name="viewport" content="width=device-width"&gt;<br>    &lt;title&gt;{{config.site_title}}&lt;/title&gt;<br>    &lt;link rel="stylesheet" href="https://maxcdn.bootstrapcdn.com/bootstrap/3.3.7/css/bootstrap.min.css" /&gt;<br>    {{#if ENV_DEVELOPMENT}}<br>      &lt;script src="http://localhost:35729/livereload.js"&gt;&lt;/script&gt;<br>    {{/if}}<br>    &lt;script src="https://js.stripe.com/v3/"&gt;&lt;/script&gt;</pre>
           <pre name="b7a3" id="b7a3" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--pre">  &lt;/head&gt;<br>  &lt;body&gt;<br><br></pre>
           <pre name="010a" id="010a" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--pre">  {{{body}}}</pre>
           <pre name="5155" id="5155" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--pre">  &lt;script<br>    src="https://code.jquery.com/jquery-3.2.1.min.js"<br>    integrity="sha256-hwg4gsxgFZhOsEEamdOYGBf13FyQuiTwlAQgxVSNgt4="<br>    crossorigin="anonymous"&gt;&lt;/script&gt;<br>  &lt;script src="https://maxcdn.bootstrapcdn.com/bootstrap/3.3.7/js/bootstrap.min.js"&gt;&lt;/script&gt;<br>  &lt;/body&gt;<br>&lt;/html&gt;</pre>
           <p name="7106" id="7106" class="graf graf--p graf-after--pre"><strong class="markup--strong markup--p-strong">The Header Partial:</strong></p>
           <p name="b1cb" id="b1cb" class="graf graf--p graf-after--p">Handlebars expects partials to be found in the <code class="markup--code markup--p-code">/views/partials</code> directory by default so we'll make <code class="markup--code markup--p-code">header.handlebars</code> there. It will look like this:</p>
           <pre name="a15e" id="a15e" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--p">&lt;header&gt;<br>  &lt;div class="container"&gt;<br>    &lt;div class="row"&gt;<br>      &lt;div class="col-xs-12 text-center"&gt;<br>        &lt;h1&gt;{{config.site_title}}&lt;/h1&gt;<br>      &lt;/div&gt;<br>    &lt;/div&gt;<br>  &lt;/div&gt;<br>&lt;/header&gt;</pre>
           <pre name="9b2c" id="9b2c" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--pre">&lt;nav class="navbar navbar-default"&gt;<br>  &lt;div class="container-fluid"&gt;<br>    &lt;div class="navbar-header"&gt;<br>      &lt;button type="button" class="navbar-toggle collapsed" data-toggle="collapse" data-target="#navbar-collapse-header" aria-expanded="false"&gt;<br>        &lt;span class="sr-only"&gt;Toggle navigation&lt;/span&gt;<br>        &lt;span class="icon-bar"&gt;&lt;/span&gt;<br>        &lt;span class="icon-bar"&gt;&lt;/span&gt;<br>        &lt;span class="icon-bar"&gt;&lt;/span&gt;<br>      &lt;/button&gt;<br>    &lt;/div&gt;</pre>
           <pre name="71ab" id="71ab" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--pre">    &lt;div class="collapse navbar-collapse" id="navbar-collapse-header"&gt;<br>      &lt;ul class="nav navbar-nav"&gt;<br>        &lt;li {{#if route_posts}}class="active"{{/if}}&gt;&lt;a href="/posts"&gt;Posts&lt;span class="sr-only"&gt;(current)&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/li&gt;<br>        &lt;li&gt;&lt;a href="/premium"&gt;Premium Content&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/li&gt;<br>      &lt;/ul&gt;<br>      &lt;ul class="nav navbar-nav navbar-right"&gt;<br>        {{#if logged_in}}<br>          &lt;li class="navbar-text text-center"&gt;Welcome Back, {{user.first_name}}!&lt;/li&gt;<br>          &lt;li&gt;&lt;a href="/logout"&gt;Logout&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/li&gt;<br>        {{/if}}</pre>
           <pre name="5846" id="5846" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--pre">        {{#unless logged_in}}<br>          &lt;li {{#if route_login}}class="active"{{/if}}&gt;&lt;a href="/login"&gt;Login&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/li&gt;<br>          &lt;li {{#if route_signup}}class="active"{{/if}}&gt;&lt;a href="/plans"&gt;Sign Up&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/li&gt;<br>        {{/unless}}<br>      &lt;/ul&gt;<br>    &lt;/div&gt;<br>  &lt;/div&gt;<br>&lt;/nav&gt;</pre>
           <p name="7797" id="7797" class="graf graf--p graf-after--pre"><strong class="markup--strong markup--p-strong">Note:</strong> In the header partial we take advantage of Handlebars’ built in <code class="markup--code markup--p-code">if</code> and <code class="markup--code markup--p-code">unless</code>helpers to make parts of our code route-specific. The we'll pass the relative booleans later in the route handlers.</p>
           <p name="21ff" id="21ff" class="graf graf--p graf-after--p"><strong class="markup--strong markup--p-strong">The Posts View</strong></p>
           <p name="59bd" id="59bd" class="graf graf--p graf-after--p">On the Posts page we want to:</p>
           <ol class="postList">
            <li name="e81a" id="e81a" class="graf graf--li graf-after--p">Display the header</li>
            <li name="1a73" id="1a73" class="graf graf--li graf-after--li">Show an error message if the user is trying to access premium posts without an account</li>
            <li name="d35f" id="d35f" class="graf graf--li graf-after--li">Abstract the post display logic to it’s own partial to make our code cleaner and modular.</li>
           </ol>
           <p name="fc09" id="fc09" class="graf graf--p graf-after--li">For the error message, we’ll rely on Handlebars’ <code class="markup--code markup--p-code">if</code> helper as we did before. For showing summaries of the posts, we'll be passing the posts to the view as an array of post objects. This lets us use the Handlebars <code class="markup--code markup--p-code">each</code> block helper to iterate over that array (each post being accessible as <code class="markup--code markup--p-code">this</code>). Our Posts view will then look like this:</p>
           <pre name="d31a" id="d31a" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--p">{{&gt; header}}<br>&lt;div class="container"&gt;<br>  &lt;div class="row"&gt;<br>    {{#if error}}<br>      &lt;div class="alert alert-danger" role="alert"&gt;<br>        {{error}}<br>      &lt;/div&gt;<br>    {{/if}}<br>    {{#each posts}}<br>      {{&gt; post-container this}}<br>    {{/each}}<br>  &lt;/div&gt;<br>&lt;/div&gt;</pre>
           <p name="af08" id="af08" class="graf graf--p graf-after--pre"><strong class="markup--strong markup--p-strong">The Post Container partial:</strong></p>
           <p name="8b03" id="8b03" class="graf graf--p graf-after--p">The next obvious step is to build the container to show summaries of each post on the Posts page. Beyond displaying the post’s title and content (which is easily accessed with <code class="markup--code markup--p-code">this.title</code>, etc.) we want to show the user if the post is premium, as well as a truncation of the post's body and it's creation date.</p>
           <p name="b9c7" id="b9c7" class="graf graf--p graf-after--p">We’ll again turn to the <code class="markup--code markup--p-code">if</code> helper to show a star beside the post if <code class="markup--code markup--p-code">this.metadata.premium</code>returns <code class="markup--code markup--p-code">true</code>, which is simple enough. For the blurb and creation date, we need to modify the <code class="markup--code markup--p-code">content</code> and <code class="markup--code markup--p-code">created_at</code> properties of the Post object; in the first place, to shorten it, in the latter, because Cosmic stores the date in ISO datetime format. To keep display logic out of our views, Handlebars provides us with functionality to write own helpers.</p>
           <p name="f097" id="f097" class="graf graf--p graf-after--p">First, get the view code in place:</p>
           <pre name="b343" id="b343" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--p">&lt;!-- /views/partials/post-container.handlebars --&gt;</pre>
           <pre name="5911" id="5911" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--pre">&lt;div style="border-bottom: 3px solid #337ab7" class="col-xs-12 col-md-8 col-md-offset-2"&gt;<br>  &lt;h2&gt;<br>    {{#if this.metadata.premium}}<br>      &lt;span style="font-size: 0.5em" class="glyphicon glyphicon-star"&gt;&lt;/span&gt;<br>    {{/if}}<br>    &lt;a href="/post/{{this.slug}}"&gt;{{this.title}}&lt;/a&gt;<br>  &lt;/h2&gt;<br>  &lt;p style="margin: 35px 40px"&gt;<br>    {{truncateText this.content 20}} &lt;a href="/post/{{this.slug}}"&gt;Read more&lt;/a&gt;<br>  &lt;/p&gt;<br>  &lt;em style="margin: 20px 0" class="pull-right"&gt;<br>    {{date this.created_at}}<br>  &lt;/em&gt;<br>&lt;/div&gt;</pre>
           <p name="a9e6" id="a9e6" class="graf graf--p graf-after--pre">(Hint: our handlebars helpers will be named <em class="markup--em markup--p-em">truncateText</em> and <em class="markup--em markup--p-em">date</em>.)</p>
           <p name="455c" id="455c" class="graf graf--p graf-after--p">Open <code class="markup--code markup--p-code">app.js</code> and find the snippet of code that sets Handlebars as the view engine. <code class="markup--code markup--p-code">exphbs</code>is a reference to <code class="markup--code markup--p-code">express-handlebars</code> and the object passed to it contains the parameters used to instantiate the engine. We need to add the <code class="markup--code markup--p-code">helpers</code> property to that object. The <code class="markup--code markup--p-code">helpers</code> property will then point to the <code class="markup--code markup--p-code">date</code> and <code class="markup--code markup--p-code">truncateText</code>methods as follows:</p>
           <pre name="2374" id="2374" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--p">// app.js</pre>
           <pre name="4734" id="4734" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--pre">// etc...<br>app.engine('handlebars', exphbs({<br>  defaultLayout: 'main',<br>  partialsDir: ['views/partials/'],<br>  helpers: {<br>    date: function(date) {<br>      return dateFormat(new Date(date), "dddd, mmmm dS, yyyy")<br>    },<br>    truncateText: function(text, length) {<br>      return truncate(text, length, { stripTags: true, byWords: true })<br>    }<br>  }<br>}));<br>app.set('views', path.join(__dirname, 'views'));<br>app.set('view engine', 'handlebars');<br>// etc...</pre>
           <p name="0390" id="0390" class="graf graf--p graf-after--pre">To illustrate, <code class="markup--code markup--p-code">{{truncateText this.content 20}}</code> tells Handlebars to render the result of <code class="markup--code markup--p-code">truncate(this.content, 20, {...} )</code>&nbsp;.</p>
           <p name="acf0" id="acf0" class="graf graf--p graf-after--p"><strong class="markup--strong markup--p-strong">The Post View:</strong></p>
           <p name="d626" id="d626" class="graf graf--p graf-after--p">Our users need to be able to read individual posts, so we’ll build a simple view that get’s passed an array that’s one post long. (In the future, outside the scope of this guide, we may find it useful to use the view to display multiple full posts in succession.)</p>
           <p name="4342" id="4342" class="graf graf--p graf-after--p">We’ll also display an error if the post isn’t found. Create your post view like so:</p>
           <pre name="e05f" id="e05f" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--p">&lt;!-- /views/post.handlebars --&gt;</pre>
           <pre name="705d" id="705d" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--pre">{{&gt; header}}<br>{{#if not_found}}<br>  &lt;div class="container"&gt;<br>    &lt;div class="row text-center"&gt;<br>      &lt;div class="col-xs12 col-md-6 col-md-offset-3"&gt;<br>        &lt;div class="alert alert-danger"&gt;<br>          Post Not Found!<br>        &lt;/div&gt;<br>        &lt;a href="/posts"&gt;See All Posts&lt;/a&gt;<br>      &lt;/div&gt;<br>    &lt;/div&gt;<br>  &lt;/div&gt;<br>{{/if}}</pre>
           <pre name="8608" id="8608" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--pre">{{#each post}}<br>  &lt;article class="container"&gt;<br>    &lt;div class="row"&gt;<br>      &lt;div class="col-xs-12 col-sm-8 col-sm-offset-2"&gt;<br>        &lt;h1&gt;{{this.title}}&lt;/h1&gt;<br>        &lt;div class="lead" style="font-size: 1.5em"&gt;<br>          {{{this.content}}}<br>        &lt;/div&gt;<br>        &lt;em class="pull-right"&gt;<br>          &lt;time&gt;{{date this.created_at}}&lt;/time&gt;<br>        &lt;/em&gt;<br>      &lt;/div&gt;<br>    &lt;/div&gt;<br>  &lt;/article&gt;<br>{{/each}}</pre>
           <p name="3499" id="3499" class="graf graf--p graf-after--pre"><strong class="markup--strong markup--p-strong">The Login Page:</strong></p>
           <p name="fb6b" id="fb6b" class="graf graf--p graf-after--p">The login page will be the simplest yet?—?a basic form that POSTs to a login route.</p>
           <pre name="994c" id="994c" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--p">&lt;!-- /views/login.handlebars --&gt;</pre>
           <pre name="c0b0" id="c0b0" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--pre">{{&gt; header}}</pre>
           <pre name="adf1" id="adf1" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--pre">&lt;div class="container"&gt;<br>  &lt;div class="row"&gt;<br>    &lt;div class="col-xs-12 col-sm-4 col-sm-offset-4"&gt;<br>      &lt;h1&gt;Log In&lt;/h1&gt;<br>      &lt;p class="text-muted"&gt;<br>        Log in to view premium content.<br>      &lt;/p&gt;</pre>
           <pre name="6527" id="6527" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--pre">      &lt;form method="post"&gt;<br>        &lt;input class="form-control" type="email" name="email" placeholder="Email" required/&gt;<br>        &lt;input type="password" class="form-control" name="password" placeholder="Password" required /&gt;<br>        &lt;button class="btn btn-lg btn-primary btn-block submit-btn" type="submit"&gt;Log in&lt;/button&gt;<br>      &lt;/form&gt;<br>    &lt;/div&gt;<br>  &lt;/div&gt;<br>&lt;/div&gt;</pre>
           <pre name="517a" id="517a" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--pre">&lt;style&gt;<br>  form &gt; input, button {<br>    margin-top: 12px;<br>  }<br>&lt;/style&gt;</pre>
           <p name="af76" id="af76" class="graf graf--p graf-after--pre"><strong class="markup--strong markup--p-strong">The Plans Page:</strong></p>
           <p name="cf83" id="cf83" class="graf graf--p graf-after--p">Obviously, our users will need to be able to signup before they can login, but since we’re giving them the option to choose one of three subscription plans we’ll build out a view that shows them their options just before checking out. Later, we’ll need to pass the Subscriptions object to this view so we can set the plan prices from Cosmic, rather than hard coding them. The view will look like this:</p>
           <pre name="8f54" id="8f54" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--p">&lt;!-- /views/plans.handlebars --&gt;</pre>
           <pre name="326f" id="326f" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--pre">{{&gt; header}}</pre>
           <pre name="bba3" id="bba3" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--pre">&lt;div class="container"&gt;<br>  &lt;div class="row text-center lead"&gt;<br>    &lt;h1&gt;Choose a Plan to Read Premium Content&lt;/h1&gt;<br>    &lt;p&gt;<br>      Sign up to view Premium Content on {{config.site_title}}<br>    &lt;/p&gt;<br>  &lt;/div&gt;</pre>
           <pre name="c8ac" id="c8ac" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--pre">  &lt;div class="row"&gt;<br>    &lt;div class="col-sm-4"&gt;<br>      &lt;h3 class="text-center text-muted"&gt;<br> &lt;span class="glyphicon glyphicon-ok text-success"&gt;&lt;/span&gt;Here's a good benefit<br>        &lt;/li&gt;<br>        &lt;li&gt;<br>          &lt;span class="glyphicon glyphicon-ok text-success"&gt;&lt;/span&gt;A reason to buy<br>        &lt;/li&gt;<br>        &lt;li&gt;<br>          &lt;span class="glyphicon glyphicon-ok text-success"&gt;&lt;/span&gt;Why you have to have it<br>        &lt;/li&gt;<br>        &lt;li&gt;<br>          &lt;span class="glyphicon glyphicon-ok text-success"&gt;&lt;/span&gt;Why you shouldn't miss out<br>        &lt;/li&gt;<br>        &lt;li&gt;<br>          &lt;span class="glyphicon glyphicon-ok text-success"&gt;&lt;/span&gt;Believe it.<br>        &lt;/li&gt;<br>      &lt;/ul&gt;<br>      &lt;a href="/signup?plan=monthly"&gt;&lt;button class="btn months&lt;/strong&gt;<br>      &lt;/p&gt;<br>      &lt;h1 class="text-center text-success"&gt;{{subscriptions.yearly_price}}&lt;/h1&gt;<br>        &lt;ul class="list-unstyled lead" style="padding: 0
