shouldn't miss out<br>          &lt;/li&gt;<br>          &lt;li&gt;<br>            &lt;span class="glyphicon glyphicon-ok text-success"&gt;&lt;/span&gt;Believe it.<br>          &lt;/li&gt;<br>        &lt;/ul&gt;<br>        &lt;a href="/signup?plan=yearly"&gt;&lt;button class="btn btn-block btn-default btn-lg"&gt;Sign Up&lt;/button&gt;&lt;/a&gt;<br>    &lt;/div&gt;<br>    &lt;div class="col-sm-4"&gt;<br>      &lt;h3 class="text-center text-muted"&gt;<br>        Quarterly<br>      &lt;/h3&gt;<br>      &lt;p class="text-center"&gt;<br>        &lt;strong&gt;Billed every 3 months&lt;/strong&gt;<br>      &lt;/p&gt;<br>      &lt;h1 class="text-center text-success"&gt;{{subscriptions.quarterly_price}}&lt;/h1 class="text-center text-success"&gt;<br>        &lt;ul class="list-unstyled lead" style="padding: 0 30px"&gt;<br>          &lt;li&gt;<br>            &lt;span class="glyphicon glyphicon-ok text-success"&gt;&lt;/span&gt;Here's a good benefit<br>          &lt;/li&gt;<br>          &lt;li&gt;<br>            &lt;span class="glyphicon glyphicon-ok text-success"&gt;&lt;/span&gt;A reason to buy<br>          &lt;/li&gt;<br>          &lt;li&gt;<br>            &lt;span class="glyphicon glyphicon-ok text-success"&gt;&lt;/span&gt;Why you have to have it<br>          &lt;/li&gt;<br>          &lt;li&gt;<br>            &lt;span class="glyphicon glyphicon-ok text-success"&gt;&lt;/span&gt;Why you shouldn't miss out<br>          &lt;/li&gt;<br>          &lt;li&gt;<br>            &lt;span class="glyphicon glyphicon-ok text-success"&gt;&lt;/span&gt;Believe it.<br>          &lt;/li&gt;<br>        &lt;/ul&gt;<br>        &lt;a href="/signup?plan=quarterly"&gt;&lt;button class="btn btn-block btn-default btn-lg"&gt;Sign Up&lt;/button&gt;&lt;/a&gt;<br>    &lt;/div&gt;<br>  &lt;/div&gt;<br>&lt;/div&gt;</pre>
           <pre name="7fb4" id="7fb4" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--pre">&lt;style&gt;<br>  form &gt; input, button {<br>    margin-top: 12px;<br>  }<br>  ul.lead {<br>    margin-top: 40px<br>  }<br>  .lead &gt; li {<br>    margin: 8px 0<br>  }<br>  .glyphicon {<br>    margin-right: 12px<br>  }<br>  .btn {<br>    margin: 35px 0px;<br>  }<br>&lt;/style&gt;</pre>
           <p name="8981" id="8981" class="graf graf--p graf-after--pre"><em class="markup--em markup--p-em">Notice that each Sign Up button links to the </em><code class="markup--code markup--p-code"><em class="markup--em markup--p-em">signup</em></code><em class="markup--em markup--p-em"> route, passing a query paramter associated with the plan selected. I.e. </em><code class="markup--code markup--p-code"><em class="markup--em markup--p-em">/signup?plan={:plan}</em></code></p>
           <p name="182f" id="182f" class="graf graf--p graf-after--p"><strong class="markup--strong markup--p-strong">The Signup Page:</strong></p>
           <p name="a434" id="a434" class="graf graf--p graf-after--p">Last, but certainly not least?—?the money maker. We’ve saved our most complicated view for last. These are our requirements:</p>
           <ol class="postList">
            <li name="d8e5" id="d8e5" class="graf graf--li graf-after--p">We need to pass the plan chosen on the page before in <code class="markup--code markup--li-code">planName</code>. (Later we'll do this in a URL query string)</li>
            <li name="822f" id="822f" class="graf graf--li graf-after--li">We need to use the Stripe Elements API for collecting credit card information. This is what we included <code class="markup--code markup--li-code">Stripe.js</code> in the Main layout earlier. At the end of our checkout form we need two <code class="markup--code markup--li-code">div</code>s; one ID'd <code class="markup--code markup--li-code">card-element</code> and the other ID'd <code class="markup--code markup--li-code">card-errors</code> for <code class="markup--code markup--li-code">Stripe.js</code> to inject into after the initial DOM rendering.</li>
            <li name="ebb4" id="ebb4" class="graf graf--li graf-after--li">We need to pass our publishable stripe key to make it all work.</li>
           </ol>
           <p name="b6d6" id="b6d6" class="graf graf--p graf-after--li">Starting with the HTML we have:</p>
           <pre name="cc45" id="cc45" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--p">&lt;!-- /views/signup.handlebars --&gt;<br>{{&gt;header}}</pre>
           <pre name="d4a4" id="d4a4" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--pre">&lt;div class="container"&gt;<br>  &lt;div class="row"&gt;<br>    &lt;form method="post" id="payment-form"&gt;<br>      &lt;div class="col-xs-12 text-center"&gt;<br>        &lt;h4 class="lead"&gt;&lt;em&gt;You're one step away from a &lt;u&gt;{{planName}}&lt;/u&gt; subscription to {{config.site_title}}!&lt;/em&gt;&lt;/h4&gt;<br>      &lt;/div&gt;<br>    &lt;/div&gt;<br>    &lt;div class="row"  style="margin-top: 30px"&gt;<br>      &lt;div class="col-md-8 col-md-offset-2"&gt;<br>        &lt;h4&gt;Enter your account details and payment information&lt;/h4&gt;</pre>
           <pre name="86f2" id="86f2" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--pre">        &lt;label for="first_name"&gt;First name:&lt;/label&gt;<br>        &lt;input type="text" name="first_name" class="form-control" placeholder="First name" required /&gt;<br>        &lt;label for="last_name"&gt;Last name:&lt;/label&gt;<br>        &lt;input type="text" name="last_name" class="form-control" placeholder="Last name" required /&gt;<br>        &lt;label for="email"&gt;Email:&lt;/label&gt;<br>        &lt;input type="email" name="email" class="form-control" placeholder="Email" required /&gt;<br>        &lt;label for="password"&gt;Password&lt;/label&gt;<br>        &lt;input type="password" name="password" class="form-control" placeholder="Password" required /&gt;<br>        &lt;label for="card-element"&gt;Credit or debit card&lt;/label&gt;<br>        &lt;div class="form-control" id="card-element"&gt;&lt;/div&gt;<br>        &lt;div id="card-errors" role="alert"&gt;&lt;/div&gt;<br>        &lt;button id="submit-button" class="btn-success btn btn-lg btn-block btn-default" &gt;Submit Payment&lt;/button&gt;</pre>
           <pre name="7ccc" id="7ccc" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--pre">      &lt;/div&gt;<br>    &lt;/div&gt;<br>    &lt;/form&gt;<br>&lt;/div&gt;</pre>
           <p name="e17d" id="e17d" class="graf graf--p graf-after--pre">Then, for simplicity, we’ll follow this with an inline script that integrates Stripe:</p>
           <pre name="0d56" id="0d56" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--p">&lt;!-- views/signup.handlebars --&gt;</pre>
           <pre name="fa19" id="fa19" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--pre">&lt;script&gt;<br>  var stripe = Stripe('{{stripeKeyPublishable}}')<br>  var elements = stripe.elements()<br>  var card = elements.create('card')<br>  var style = {<br>      base: {<br>        color: '#32325d',<br>        lineHeight: '24px',<br>        fontFamily: '"Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, sans-serif',<br>        fontSmoothing: 'antialiased',<br>        fontSize: '16px',<br>        '::placeholder': {<br>          color: '#aab7c4'<br>        }<br>      },<br>      invalid: {<br>        color: '#fa755a',<br>        iconColor: '#fa755a'<br>      }<br>    };</pre>
           <pre name="02ca" id="02ca" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--pre">  card.mount('#card-element', {style: style})</pre>
           <pre name="a544" id="a544" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--pre">  // Handle real-time validation errors from the card Element.<br>card.addEventListener('change', function(event) {<br>  var displayError = document.getElementById('card-errors');<br>  if (event.error) {<br>    displayError.textContent = event.error.message;<br>  } else {<br>    displayError.textContent = '';<br>  }<br>});</pre>
           <pre name="7871" id="7871" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--pre">// Handle form submission<br>var form = document.getElementById('payment-form');<br>var submitButton = document.getElementById('submit-button');<br>form.addEventListener('submit', function(event) {<br>  event.preventDefault();<br>  submitButton.disabled=true<br>  stripe.createToken(card).then(function(result) {<br>    if (result.error) {<br>      // Inform the user if there was an error<br>      var errorElement = document.getElementById('card-errors');<br>      errorElement.textContent = result.error.message;<br>      submitButton.disabled=false<br>    } else {<br>      // Send the token to your server<br>      stripeTokenHandler(result.token);<br>    }<br>  });<br>});</pre>
           <pre name="2f09" id="2f09" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--pre">function stripeTokenHandler(token) {<br>  // Insert the token ID into the form so it gets submitted to the server<br>  var form = document.getElementById('payment-form');<br>  var hiddenInput = document.createElement('input');<br>  hiddenInput.setAttribute('type', 'hidden');<br>  hiddenInput.setAttribute('name', 'stripeToken');<br>  hiddenInput.setAttribute('value', token.id);<br>  form.appendChild(hiddenInput);<br>  // Submit the form<br>  form.submit();<br>}<br>&lt;/script&gt;</pre>
           <pre name="c42e" id="c42e" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--pre">&lt;style&gt;<br>  label,button {<br>    margin-top: 22px;<br>  }<br>&lt;/style&gt;</pre>
           <p name="9bdd" id="9bdd" class="graf graf--p graf-after--pre">Here’s what’s going on:</p>
           <ol class="postList">
            <li name="45f8" id="45f8" class="graf graf--li graf-after--p">We instantiate Stripe with the Publishable key we passed, assign its <code class="markup--code markup--li-code">elements</code> library to it's own variable, use that to create a <code class="markup--code markup--li-code">card</code> element, and finally mount that to the <code class="markup--code markup--li-code">&lt;div id="card-element"&gt;</code> we created earlier. The card object handles card validation, comes packaged with good UX features, and reports errors back to the user in real time.</li>
            <li name="b347" id="b347" class="graf graf--li graf-after--li">We attach an event listener to the card object that responds to any change in either the user-inputted card number, CCV, or expiration date. It mounts that error on <code class="markup--code markup--li-code">&lt;div id="card-errors"&gt;</code></li>
            <li name="2c33" id="2c33" class="graf graf--li graf-after--li">We handle the form submission manually. First, we prevent the default action and disable multiple submissions. Then, barring no errors, we attach a hidden field to the form that contains Stripe’s validation token, provided by <code class="markup--code markup--li-code">Stripe.js</code>, and <em class="markup--em markup--li-em">then</em> submit the form to the <code class="markup--code markup--li-code">Signup</code> route.</li>
           </ol>
           <h3 name="f630" id="f630" class="graf graf--h3 graf-after--li">7. Build the&nbsp;Routes</h3>
           <p name="78d3" id="78d3" class="graf graf--p graf-after--h3">With our views built, we know exactly what routes our application needs. Namely:</p>
           <ul class="postList">
            <li name="9e92" id="9e92" class="graf graf--li graf-after--p">Posts</li>
            <li name="afaf" id="afaf" class="graf graf--li graf-after--li">Post</li>
            <li name="ca52" id="ca52" class="graf graf--li graf-after--li">Premium</li>
            <li name="1346" id="1346" class="graf graf--li graf-after--li">Login</li>
            <li name="2789" id="2789" class="graf graf--li graf-after--li">Logout</li>
            <li name="694d" id="694d" class="graf graf--li graf-after--li">Signup</li>
            <li name="a04f" id="a04f" class="graf graf--li graf-after--li">Plans</li>
           </ul>
           <p name="9a18" id="9a18" class="graf graf--p graf-after--li">By default, your app has a <code class="markup--code markup--p-code">Users</code> route and an <code class="markup--code markup--p-code">Index</code> route. Delete <code class="markup--code markup--p-code">Users</code> and make <code class="markup--code markup--p-code">Index</code> redirect to <code class="markup--code markup--p-code">Posts</code> like so:</p>
           <pre name="5fb9" id="5fb9" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--p">// /routes/index.js</pre>
           <pre name="cdcf" id="cdcf" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--pre">var express = require('express')<br>var router = express.Router()</pre>
           <pre name="ba10" id="ba10" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--pre">router.get('/', function(req, res) {<br>  res.redirect('/posts')<br>});</pre>
           <pre name="467f" id="467f" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--pre">module.exports = router</pre>
           <p name="9ede" id="9ede" class="graf graf--p graf-after--pre"><strong class="markup--strong markup--p-strong">The Posts Route:</strong></p>
           <p name="3ab1" id="3ab1" class="graf graf--p graf-after--p">Posts will use <code class="markup--code markup--p-code">async</code> to string together a series of async functions: one using the Cosmic JS client to get our Posts, the next using Cosmic to get the site config and render the <code class="markup--code markup--p-code">posts</code>view, passing in the relevant locals. If the user is not in an authenticated session, we'll use <code class="markup--code markup--p-code">lodash</code> to filter out the posts returned from Cosmic which <em class="markup--em markup--p-em">have not</em> been labelled premium (and are therefore free to read). We'll pass the Posts, Config, and route-specific view data via <code class="markup--code markup--p-code">res.locals</code>.</p>
           <pre name="b6f4" id="b6f4" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--p">var express = require('express');<br>var router = express.Router();<br>var cosmic = require('cosmicjs');<br>var async = require('async');<br>var _ = require('lodash')</pre>
           <pre name="513a" id="513a" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--pre">router.get('/', function(req, res) {<br>  async.series([<br>    function(cb) {<br>      cosmic.getObjectType(req.app.locals.config, { type_slug: 'posts' }, function(err, response) {<br>        (req.session.user) ? res.locals.posts = response.objects.all : res.locals.posts = _.filter(response.objects.all, function(post) {<br>          return !post.metadata.premium<br>        })<br>        cb()<br>      })<br>    },<br>    function(cb) {<br>      cosmic.getObject(req.app.locals.config, { slug: 'site' }, function(err, response) {<br>        res.locals.config = response.object.metadata<br>        res.locals.user = req.session.user<br>        res.locals.route_posts = true<br>        if (req.session.user) res.locals.logged_in = true<br>        return res.render('posts.handlebars')<br>      })=<br>    }<br>  ])<br>});</pre>
           <pre name="cc77" id="cc77" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--pre">module.exports = router;</pre>
           <p name="7bcd" id="7bcd" class="graf graf--p graf-after--pre"><strong class="markup--strong markup--p-strong">The Post Route:</strong></p>
           <p name="422b" id="422b" class="graf graf--p graf-after--p">Having a route for all posts, we’ll need a companion route for a singular post that takes the post slug as a URL parameter and returns that post if it’s found, utilizing similar logic as the <code class="markup--code markup--p-code">Posts</code> route.</p>
           <pre name="9511" id="9511" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--p">// routes/post.js</pre>
           <pre name="5ec9" id="5ec9" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--pre">var express = require('express');<br>var router = express.Router();<br>var cosmic = require('cosmicjs');<br>var async = require('async');<br>var _ = require('lodash')</pre>
           <pre name="7f4a" id="7f4a" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--pre">router.get('/:slug', function(req, res) {<br>  async.series([<br>    function(cb) {<br>      cosmic.getObjectType(req.app.locals.config, { type_slug: 'posts' }, function(err, response) {<br>        res.locals.post = _.filter(response.objects.all, function(post) {<br>          return post.slug === req.params.slug<br>        })<br>        if (!res.locals.post) res.locals.not_found = true<br>        cb()<br>      })<br>    },<br>    function(cb) {<br>      cosmic.getObject(req.app.locals.config, { slug: 'site' }, function(err, response) {<br>        res.locals.config = response.object.metadata<br>        res.locals.user = req.session.user<br>        return res.render('post.handlebars')<br>      })<br>    }<br>  ])<br>});</pre>
           <pre name="cd1f" id="cd1f" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--pre">module.exports = router</pre>
           <p name="1fa5" id="1fa5" class="graf graf--p graf-after--pre"><strong class="markup--strong markup--p-strong">The Login Route:</strong></p>
           <p name="21c0" id="21c0" class="graf graf--p graf-after--p">To let users have access to premium posts, we’ll need to collect their login information, hash their password with bcrypt, and check it against the password associated with the email address stored in Cosmic.</p>
           <p name="e312" id="e312" class="graf graf--p graf-after--p">A GET request will render the login form. We then handle the form’s POST request by retrieiving all users from Cosmic and iteratating over all users with a series of two async functions: one using bcrypt to compare password hashes, the next saving the user’s data into a session if they’re found.</p>
           <pre name="4d47" id="4d47" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--p">// routes/login.js</pre>
           <pre name="9cfb" id="9cfb" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--pre">var express = require('express');<br>var router = express.Router();<br>var cosmic = require('cosmicjs');<br>var async = require('async');<br>var _ = require('lodash')<br>var bcrypt = require('bcrypt')</pre>
           <pre name="8668" id="8668" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--pre">router.get('/', function(req, res) {<br>  async.series([<br>    function(cb) {<br>      cosmic.getObject(req.app.locals.config, { slug: 'site' }, function(err, response) {<br>        res.locals.config = response.object.metadata<br>        res.locals.route_login = true<br>        return res.render('login.handlebars')<br>      })<br>    }<br>  ])<br>});</pre>
           <pre name="3a81" id="3a81" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--pre">router.post('/', function(req, res) {<br>  cosmic.getObjectType(req.app.locals.config, { type_slug: 'users' }, function (err, response) {<br>    if (err) res.status(500).json({ status: 'error', data: response })<br>    else {<br>      async.eachSeries(response.objects.all, function (user, eachCb) {<br>        if (!_.find(user.metafields, { key: 'email', value: req.body.email.trim().toLowerCase() }))<br>          return eachCb()<br>        const stored_password = _.find(user.metafields, { key: 'password' }).value<br>        bcrypt.compare(req.body.password, stored_password, function (err, correct) {<br>          if (correct) res.locals.user_found = user<br>          eachCb()<br>        })<br>      }, function () {<br>        if (res.locals.user_found) {<br>          req.session.user = {<br>            first_name: res.locals.user_found.metafield.first_name.value,<br>            last_name: res.locals.user_found.metafield.last_name.value,<br>            email: res.locals.user_found.metafield.email.value<br>          }<br>          req.session.save()<br>          return res.redirect('/posts')<br>        }<br>        return res.status(404).json({ status: 'error', message: 'User not found' })<br>      })<br>    }<br>  })<br>})</pre>
           <pre name="6543" id="6543" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--pre">module.exports = router</pre>
           <p name="ff3f" id="ff3f" class="graf graf--p graf-after--pre"><strong class="markup--strong markup--p-strong">The Plans Route:</strong></p>
           <p name="ed12" id="ed12" class="graf graf--p graf-after--p">Before a user can log in, we need a sign up form so we can have users in the first place. As said before, we’ll show them their subscription options right before the signup form. This does nothing more than pass the Site and Subscription configs before rendering the view:</p>
           <pre name="1423" id="1423" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--p">var express = require('express');<br>var router = express.Router();<br>var cosmic = require('cosmicjs');<br>var async = require('async')</pre>
           <pre name="8bcb" id="8bcb" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--pre">router.get('/', function(req, res) {<br>  async.series([<br>    function(cb) {<br>      cosmic.getObject(req.app.locals.config, { slug: 'site' }, function(err, response) {<br>        res.locals.config = response.object.metadata<br>        res.locals.route_signup = true<br>        cb()<br>      })<br>    },<br>    function(cb) {<br>      cosmic.getObject(req.app.locals.config, { slug: 'subscriptions' }, function(err, response) {<br>        res.locals.subscriptions = response.object.metadata<br>        res.render('plans.handlebars')<br>      })<br>    }<br>  ])<br>});</pre>
           <pre name="7755" id="7755" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--pre">module.exports = router;</pre>
           <p name="4c8a" id="4c8a" class="graf graf--p graf-after--pre"><strong class="markup--strong markup--p-strong">The Signup Route:</strong></p>
           <p name="7e21" id="7e21" class="graf graf--p graf-after--p">As you might have guessed, the signup route has the most going on out of them all. Here’s what we need to implement:</p>
           <ol class="postList">
            <li name="9d14" id="9d14" class="graf graf--li graf-after--p">On a GET request, render the signup form and pass our publishable Stripe key through <code class="markup--code markup--li-code">res.locals</code> for Stripe.js to work.</li>
            <li name="19cd" id="19cd" class="graf graf--li graf-after--li">On a Post request:</li>
            <li name="a506" id="a506" class="graf graf--li graf-after--li">Instantiate Stripe server-side with our secret key</li>
            <li name="86fc" id="86fc" class="graf graf--li graf-after--li">If a user’s already logged in, redirect them.</li>
            <li name="563f" id="563f" class="graf graf--li graf-after--li">Run a series of two <em class="markup--em markup--li-em">named</em> async functions (so we can use their return values after both have completed) to fetch our subscription data from Cosmic and hash the password.</li>
            <li name="d14a" id="d14a" class="graf graf--li graf-after--li">Having completed Step 3, we use the Stripe API to create a new customer, associating their payment method via the Stripe token we passed from the signup form.</li>
            <li name="e895" id="e895" class="graf graf--li graf-after--li">We then charge that customer based on the plan selected and create a new subscription (again, via Stripe) so recurring payments are processed automatically.</li>
            <li name="998a" id="998a" class="graf graf--li graf-after--li">We create a new User object based on our Cosmic schema, add that to our bucket, and once that’s succesful we create a new session for the user and redirect them to the <code class="markup--code markup--li-code">Posts</code> route, where they'll now be able to view premium content.</li>
           </ol>
           <p name="3de8" id="3de8" class="graf graf--p graf-after--li">All complete, it will look like this:</p>
           <pre name="a710" id="a710" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--p">// routes/signup.js</pre>
           <pre name="50de" id="50de" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--pre">var express = require('express');<br>var router = express.Router();<br>var cosmic = require('cosmicjs');<br>var async = require('async');<br>var bcrypt = require('bcrypt')</pre>
           <pre name="0bab" id="0bab" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--pre">router.get('/', function(req, res) {<br>  if (req.session.user) res.redirect('/')<br>  async.series([<br>    function(cb) {<br>      cosmic.getObject(req.app.locals.config, { slug: 'site' }, function(err, response) {<br>        res.locals.config = response.object.metadata<br>        res.locals.route_signup = true<br>        cb()<br>      })<br>    },<br>    function(cb) {<br>      cosmic.getObject(req.app.locals.config, { slug: 'subscriptions' }, function(err, response) {<br>        res.locals.subscriptions = response.object.metadata<br>        res.locals.stripeKeyPublishable = req.app.locals.stripeKeyPublishable<br>        res.locals.planName = req.query.plan<br>        res.render('signup.handlebars')<br>      })<br>    }<br>  ])<br>});</pre>
           <pre name="fd5c" id="fd5c" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--pre">router.post('/', function(req, res) {<br>  var stripe = require('stripe')(req.app.locals.stripeKeySecret)<br>  if (req.session.user) res.redirect('/')</pre>
           <pre name="1ff3" id="1ff3" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--pre">  async.series({<br>    subscriptions: function(callback) {<br>      cosmic.getObject(req.app.locals.config, { slug: 'subscriptions' }, function(err, response) {<br>        callback(null, response.object.metadata)<br>      })<br>    },<br>    hash: function (callback) {<br>      bcrypt.hash(req.body.password, 10, function (err, hash) {<br>        callback(null, hash)<br>      })<br>    }<br>  }, function (err, results) {</pre>
           <pre name="938d" id="938d" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--pre">    stripe.customers.create({<br>      email: req.body.email,<br>      source: req.body.stripeToken<br>    }).then(function (customer) {<br>      return stripe.charges.create({<br>        amount: results.subscriptions[req.query.plan + "_price"].replace(/[$]/,'') + '00',<br>        currency: "usd",<br>        customer: customer.id<br>      })<br>    }).then(function (charge) {<br>      stripe.subscriptions.create({<br>        customer: charge.customer,<br>        items: [<br>          {<br>            plan: 'subscription-' + req.query.plan<br>          }<br>        ]<br>      })<br>      var object = {<br>        type_slug: 'users',<br>        title: req.body.first_name + ' ' + req.body.last_name,<br>        metafields: [<br>          {<br>            title: 'First name',<br>            key: 'first_name',<br>            type: 'text',<br>            value: req.body.first_name<br>          },<br>          {<br>            title: 'Last name',<br>            key: 'last_name',<br>            type: 'text',<br>            value: req.body.last_name<br>          },<br>          {<br>            title: 'Password',<br>            key: 'password',<br>            type: 'text',<br>            value: results.hash<br>          },<br>          {<br>            title: 'Email',<br>            key: 'email',<br>            type: 'text',<br>            value: req.body.email<br>          },<br>          {<br>            title: 'Stripe Id',<br>            key: 'stripe_id',<br>            type: 'text',<br>            value: charge.customer<br>          },<br>          {<br>            title: 'Subscription Type',<br>            key: 'subscription_type',<br>            type: 'text',<br>            value: req.query.plan<br>          }<br>        ]<br>      }<br>      if (req.app.locals.config.bucket.write_key) object.write_key = req.app.locals.config.bucket.write_key<br>      cosmic.addObject(req.app.locals.config, object, function (err, reponse) {<br>        if (err)<br>          res.status(500).json({ data: reponse })<br>        else {<br>          req.session.user = {<br>            first_name: req.body.first_name,<br>            last_name: req.body.last_name,<br>            email: req.body.email<br>          }<br>          req.session.save()<br>          res.redirect('/posts')<br>        }<br>      })<br>    })<br>  })<br>})</pre>
           <pre name="faee" id="faee" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--pre">module.exports = router</pre>
           <p name="817e" id="817e" class="graf graf--p graf-after--pre"><strong class="markup--strong markup--p-strong">The Logout Route:</strong></p>
           <p name="da75" id="da75" class="graf graf--p graf-after--p">To be user friendly we’ll need to give our users a chance to log out. All this requires is a POST request to <code class="markup--code markup--p-code">/logout</code>and a quick <code class="markup--code markup--p-code">session.destroy()</code> call.</p>
           <pre name="092e" id="092e" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--p">var express = require('express')<br>var router = express.Router()</pre>
           <pre name="222d" id="222d" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--pre">/* GET home page. */</pre>
           <pre name="cf63" id="cf63" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--pre">router.get('/', function(req, res) {<br>  req.session.destroy()<br>  return res.redirect('/')<br>});</pre>
           <pre name="d281" id="d281" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--pre">module.exports = router</pre>
           <p name="f2d0" id="f2d0" class="graf graf--p graf-after--pre"><strong class="markup--strong markup--p-strong">Wiring Them All Together:</strong></p>
           <p name="c20c" id="c20c" class="graf graf--p graf-after--p">Having all of our routes built and ready to work as we need them to, we’ll <code class="markup--code markup--p-code">require</code> them all in our app and point their associated enpoints to them via <code class="markup--code markup--p-code">app.use()</code></p>
           <pre name="0da0" id="0da0" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--p">// app.js</pre>
           <pre name="b297" id="b297" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--pre">var routes = require('./routes/index');<br>var posts = require('./routes/posts');<br>var post = require('./routes/post')<br>var login = require('./routes/login')<br>var logout = require('./routes/logout')<br>var signup = require('./routes/signup')<br>var plans = require('./routes/plans')<br>var premium = require('./routes/premium')<br>var api = require('./routes/api')</pre>
           <pre name="895c" id="895c" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--pre">app.use('/', routes);<br>app.use('/post', post)<br>app.use('/posts', posts)<br>app.use('/login', login)<br>app.use('/logout', logout)<br>app.use('/signup', signup)<br>app.use('/plans', plans)<br>app.use('/premium', premium)<br>app.use('/api', api)</pre>
           <p name="3cf5" id="3cf5" class="graf graf--p graf-after--pre"><strong class="markup--strong markup--p-strong">Moving On to the Extension:</strong></p>
           <p name="c802" id="c802" class="graf graf--p graf-after--p">If you’ve done everything right up until this point, your blog now works exactly as you’d expect it to. To test, go ahead and run <code class="markup--code markup--p-code">npm start</code>, create a few posts in Cosmic and verify that they're being fetched. Then create a dummy account and make sure it's being stored in Cosmic and registered by Stripe. Then, we'll build our dashboard extension for Cosmic.</p>
           <h3 name="4195" id="4195" class="graf graf--h3 graf-after--p">Part 2: Building the Extension</h3>
           <p name="f506" id="f506" class="graf graf--p graf-after--h3">Stripe provides us with an impressive amount of analytics, however we want a central location to get a quick glance at a list of all of our users, what subscription plan they’re on, and three key metrics about our blog: revenue to date, active subscriptions, and cancellations to date.</p>
           <p name="9077" id="9077" class="graf graf--p graf-after--p">Cosmic JS gives us the ability to do this by utilizing it’s extension feature, which lets us upload a SPA with <code class="markup--code markup--p-code">index.html</code> as an entry point that gets loaded into a frame in our Cosmic dashboard. Bucket keys are then provided to it via URL query strings.</p>
           <p name="c2e3" id="c2e3" class="graf graf--p graf-after--p">We’ll be building the extension with React, namely because our extension only requires a view layer.</p>
           <h3 name="3964" id="3964" class="graf graf--h3 graf-after--p">Setup</h3>
           <p name="5c41" id="5c41" class="graf graf--p graf-after--h3">To keep ourselves organized we’ll store our app under our <code class="markup--code markup--p-code">CosmicUserBlog</code> directory. Our tree will look like this:</p>
           <pre name="3c33" id="3c33" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--p"><code class="markup--code markup--pre-code">CosmicUserBlog<br>|<br>|--extensions<br>| |--subscription-management<br>| | |--client<br>| | | |--components<br>| | | |--index.js<br>| | | |--index.html<br>| | |--dist</code></pre>
           <p name="da96" id="da96" class="graf graf--p graf-after--pre">Once you have your directory structure in place, run <code class="markup--code markup--p-code">yarn init</code> and we'll move onto installaitons.</p>
           <h3 name="9dac" id="9dac" class="graf graf--h3 graf-after--p">Installations</h3>
           <p name="bd3c" id="bd3c" class="graf graf--p graf-after--h3">We need these packages:</p>
           <ul class="postList">
            <li name="7eaf" id="7eaf" class="graf graf--li graf-after--p">async</li>
            <li name="103e" id="103e" class="graf graf--li graf-after--li">axios</li>
            <li name="e0d6" id="e0d6" class="graf graf--li graf-after--li">babel-preset-2015</li>
            <li name="0018" id="0018" class="graf graf--li graf-after--li">Babel-preset-2016</li>
            <li name="b4c0" id="b4c0" class="graf graf--li graf-after--li">cosmicjs</li>
            <li name="7100" id="7100" class="graf graf--li graf-after--li">html-webpack-plugin?—?for generating our html with webpack</li>
            <li name="b262" id="b262" class="graf graf--li graf-after--li">lodash</li>
            <li name="81fa" id="81fa" class="graf graf--li graf-after--li">query-string?—?an easy way to parse bucket keys</li>
            <li name="4b6c" id="4b6c" class="graf graf--li graf-after--li">path</li>
            <li name="0c9b" id="0c9b" class="graf graf--li graf-after--li">react</li>
            <li name="54f7" id="54f7" class="graf graf--li graf-after--li">react-dom</li>
            <li name="d0a7" id="d0a7" class="graf graf--li graf-after--li">react-loading</li>
            <li name="77a9" id="77a9" class="graf graf--li graf-after--li">webpack</li>
            <li name="a8be" id="a8be" class="graf graf--li graf-after--li">babel-core</li>
            <li name="633b" id="633b" class="graf graf--li graf-after--li">babel-loader</li>
            <li name="b5cf" id="b5cf" class="graf graf--li graf-after--li">babel-preset-react</li>
           </ul>
           <p name="0233" id="0233" class="graf graf--p graf-after--li">Run <code class="markup--code markup--p-code">yarn add async axios babel-preset-2015 babel-preset-2016 cosmicjs html-webpack-plugin lodash query-string path react react-dom react-loading webpack babel-core babel-loader-babel-preset-react</code>, then we'll dive in.</p>
           <h3 name="95bb" id="95bb" class="graf graf--h3 graf-after--p">Configure Webpack and&nbsp;Babel</h3>
           <p name="e267" id="e267" class="graf graf--p graf-after--h3">First, make&nbsp;<code class="markup--code markup--p-code">.babelrc</code> in the root folder and tell it how to transpile our code:</p>
           <pre name="5a80" id="5a80" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--p">// .babelrc</pre>
           <pre name="4fb4" id="4fb4" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--pre">{<br>  "presets": [<br>    "es2016", "es2015", "react"<br>  ]<br>}</pre>
           <p name="6ec1" id="6ec1" class="graf graf--p graf-after--pre">Then, again under <code class="markup--code markup--p-code">CosmicUserBlog/extensions/subscription-management</code>, make <code class="markup--code markup--p-code">webpack.config.js</code> so we can tell Webpack how to package our modules.</p>
           <pre name="1227" id="1227" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--p">const path = require('path')<br>const HtmlWebpackPlugin = require('html-webpack-plugin')</pre>
           <pre name="3036" id="3036" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--pre">module.exports = {<br>  entry: './client/index.js',<br>  output: {<br>    path: path.resolve('dist'),<br>    filename: 'index_bundle.js'<br>  },<br>  module: {<br>    loaders: [<br>      { test: /\.js$/, loader: 'babel-loader', exclude: /node_modules/ }<br>    ]<br>  },<br>  plugins: [<br>    new HtmlWebpackPlugin({<br>      template: './client/index.html',<br>      filename: 'index.html',<br>      inject: 'body'<br>    })<br>  ]<br>}</pre>
           <p name="d6ca" id="d6ca" class="graf graf--p graf-after--pre"><code class="markup--code markup--p-code">dist</code> will contain all of our output files (those being <code class="markup--code markup--p-code">index_bundle.js</code> and <code class="markup--code markup--p-code">index.html</code>) and we'll ultimately compress <code class="markup--code markup--p-code">dist</code> to upload as our extension. html-webpack-plugin will take our html template from <code class="markup--code markup--p-code">client/index.html</code> and link to our compiled javascript in <code class="markup--code markup--p-code">dist/index.html</code> upon building.</p>
           <h3 name="a672" id="a672" class="graf graf--h3 graf-after--p">Create an Entry&nbsp;File</h3>
           <p name="a1cc" id="a1cc" class="graf graf--p graf-after--h3">We want to use Boostrap and we need a <code class="markup--code markup--p-code">div</code> (which we'll ID as <code class="markup--code markup--p-code">root</code>) for our React App to mount onto. <code class="markup--code markup--p-code">client/index.html</code> should look like this:</p>
           <pre name="a445" id="a445" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--p">&lt;!DOCTYPE html&gt;<br>&lt;html&gt;<br>  &lt;head&gt;<br>    &lt;link rel="stylesheet" href="https://maxcdn.bootstrapcdn.com/bootstrap/3.3.7/css/bootstrap.min.css" /&gt;<br>  &lt;/head&gt;<br>  &lt;body&gt;<br>    &lt;div id="root"&gt;<br>      &lt;script<br>        src="https://code.jquery.com/jquery-3.2.1.min.js"<br>        integrity="sha256-hwg4gsxgFZhOsEEamdOYGBf13FyQuiTwlAQgxVSNgt4="<br>        crossorigin="anonymous"&gt;&lt;/script&gt;<br>      &lt;script src="https://maxcdn.bootstrapcdn.com/bootstrap/3.3.7/js/bootstrap.min.js"&gt;&lt;/script&gt;<br>  &lt;/body&gt;<br>&lt;/html&gt;</pre>
           <h3 name="7003" id="7003" class="graf graf--h3 graf-after--pre">Build the React&nbsp;App</h3>
           <p name="a9ec" id="a9ec" class="graf graf--p graf-after--h3"><strong class="markup--strong markup--p-strong">1. Create an Entry Point</strong></p>
           <p name="68ff" id="68ff" class="graf graf--p graf-after--p">We have everything in place to start getting our hands dirty. We’ll use <code class="markup--code markup--p-code">client/index.js</code> as an entry point for our React app. We'll import React, set it as a global, pass our cosmic keys to it in it's props, and mount the App component (which we'll make next) to <code class="markup--code markup--p-code">&lt;div id="root"&gt;</code>.</p>
           <pre name="8fbc" id="8fbc" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--p">import React from 'react'<br>import ReactDom from 'react-dom'<br>import App from './components/App'<br>import QueryString from 'query-string'</pre>
           <pre name="37f6" id="37f6" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--pre">window.React = React<br>const url = QueryString.parse(location.search)</pre>
           <pre name="320c" id="320c" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--pre">const cosmic = { bucket: {<br>    slug: url.bucket_slug,<br>    write_key: url.write_key,<br>    read_key: url.read_key<br>  }<br>}</pre>
           <pre name="b438" id="b438" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--pre">ReactDom.render(<br>  &lt;App cosmic={cosmic}/&gt;,<br>  document.getElementById('root')<br>)</pre>
           <p name="cfbe" id="cfbe" class="graf graf--p graf-after--pre"><strong class="markup--strong markup--p-strong">2. Build the App Component</strong></p>
           <p name="d73e" id="d73e" class="graf graf--p graf-after--p">To keep our app modular, we’ll have a tiered component structure that looks like this:</p>
           <pre name="3f41" id="3f41" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--p"><code class="markup--code markup--pre-code">components<br>|<br>|--App.js<br>|--Header.js<br>|--SubscriberData<br>| |<br>| |--SubscriberContainer.js<br>| |--Loader.js<br>| |--StatsContainer.js<br>| |--StatTicker.js<br>| |--UserList.js</code></pre>
           <p name="bd00" id="bd00" class="graf graf--p graf-after--pre"><code class="markup--code markup--p-code">Header</code> and <code class="markup--code markup--p-code">SubscriberContainer</code> will be immediate children of <code class="markup--code markup--p-code">App</code>. <code class="markup--code markup--p-code">Loader</code>, <code class="markup--code markup--p-code">UserList</code>, and <code class="markup--code markup--p-code">StatsContainer</code> will all be immediate children of <code class="markup--code markup--p-code">SubcriberContainer</code>. Finally, <code class="markup--code markup--p-code">StatsContainer</code> will be composed of <code class="markup--code markup--p-code">StatTicker</code>s.</p>
           <p name="6e62" id="6e62" class="graf graf--p graf-after--p">Aside from keeping an organized project, this structure allows us to maximize our number of <em class="markup--em markup--p-em">stateless functional components</em> which are not React classes and also happen to be fast.</p>
           <p name="d90e" id="d90e" class="graf graf--p graf-after--p">Starting at the top of the heirarchy, we’ll build an App component that stores our Cosmic keys in it’s state and renders a <code class="markup--code markup--p-code">Header</code> and a <code class="markup--code markup--p-code">SubscriberContainer</code>.</p>
           <pre name="6a8f" id="6a8f" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--p">// components/App.js</pre>
           <pre name="504f" id="504f" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--pre">import { Component } from 'react'<br>import Header from './Header'<br>import SubscriberContainer from './SubscriberData/SubscriberContainer'</pre>
           <pre name="a58a" id="a58a" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--pre">export default class App extends Component {</pre>
           <pre name="e199" id="e199" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--pre">  constructor(props) {<br>    super(props)<br>    this.state = {<br>      cosmic: this.props.cosmic<br>    }<br>  }</pre>
           <pre name="5d1a" id="5d1a" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--pre">  render() {<br>    return (<br>      &lt;div&gt;<br>        &lt;Header<br>          bucket={this.state.cosmic.bucket.slug} /&gt;<br>        &lt;SubscriberContainer<br>          cosmic={this.state.cosmic} /&gt;<br>      &lt;/div&gt;<br>    )<br>  }<br>}</pre>
           <p name="2cf3" id="2cf3" class="graf graf--p graf-after--pre">The next obvious step is to build out the Header component.</p>
           <p name="b4a4" id="b4a4" class="graf graf--p graf-after--p"><strong class="markup--strong markup--p-strong">Build the Header:</strong></p>
           <p name="9dd6" id="9dd6" class="graf graf--p graf-after--p">Header will be our first stateless functional component, taking only our bucket slug as a prop:</p>
           <pre name="fb8f" id="fb8f" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--p">const Header = ({ bucket }) =&gt;<br>  &lt;nav className="navbar navbar-default"&gt;<br>    &lt;div className="container-fluid"&gt;<br>      &lt;ul className="nav navbar-nav"&gt;<br>        &lt;li className="navbar-text"&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Managing Subscriptions for: &lt;/strong&gt;&lt;em&gt;{bucket}&lt;/em&gt;&lt;/li&gt;<br>      &lt;/ul&gt;<br>    &lt;/div&gt;<br>  &lt;/nav&gt;</pre>
           <pre name="b6e8" id="b6e8" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--pre">export default Header</pre>
           <p name="aece" id="aece" class="graf graf--p graf-after--pre"><strong class="markup--strong markup--p-strong">Build the Subscriber Container:</strong></p>
           <p name="3057" id="3057" class="graf graf--p graf-after--p"><code class="markup--code markup--p-code">SubscriberContainer</code> will handle all of the logic associated with our subscriber data and render <code class="markup--code markup--p-code">StatsContainer</code> and <code class="markup--code markup--p-code">UserList</code> to display the data it processes.</p>
           <p name="bd11" id="bd11" class="graf graf--p graf-after--p"><code class="markup--code markup--p-code">SubscriberContainer</code> will be a stateful React class containing the following:</p>
           <ol class="postList">
            <li name="2dbd" id="2dbd" class="graf graf--li graf-after--p">A constructor that initializes <code class="markup--code markup--li-code">SubscriberContainer</code>'s state to contain our Cosmic keys (which we've passed as props) and reflect our subscriber data. We intialize the Revenue, Users, and Cancellations stats to <code class="markup--code markup--li-code">'Loading…'</code>and their loading state to <code class="markup--code markup--li-code">true</code>.</li>
            <li name="e204" id="e204" class="graf graf--li graf-after--li">An override for <code class="markup--code markup--li-code">componentDidMount()</code> to get our component to fetch the data we need after it mounts to the DOM, and then refresh that data every minute.</li>
            <li name="6ffb" id="6ffb" class="graf graf--li graf-after--li">A <code class="markup--code markup--li-code">getRevenue()</code> method to fetch (in an admittedly hack-ish way) our revenue by iterating over the subscription types of our active users from Cosmic and storing the calculated revenue in the state.</li>
            <li name="72cf" id="72cf" class="graf graf--li graf-after--li">A <code class="markup--code markup--li-code">getUsers()</code> method to fetch all of our users from Cosmic and store them in an array in the state, as well as their total.</li>
            <li name="0510" id="0510" class="graf graf--li graf-after--li">A <code class="markup--code markup--li-code">getCancellations()</code> method to grab the amount of cancelled subscriptions from our <code class="markup--code markup--li-code">Subscriptions</code> config object. (Later we'll be updating that number with a webhook from Stripe.)</li>
            <li name="452c" id="452c" class="graf graf--li graf-after--li">A <code class="markup--code markup--li-code">render()</code> method to render our <code class="markup--code markup--li-code">Loader</code> component (only if we're fetching data), <code class="markup--code markup--li-code">StatsContainer</code>, and <code class="markup--code markup--li-code">UserList</code>.</li>
           </ol>
           <p name="8f56" id="8f56" class="graf graf--p graf-after--li">All put together, we have this:</p>
           <pre name="10b8" id="10b8" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--p">import { Component } from 'react'<br>import Cosmic from 'cosmicjs'<br>import async from 'async'<br>import _ from 'lodash'<br>import StatsContainer from './StatsContainer'<br>import Loader from './Loader'<br>import UserList from './UserList'</pre>
           <pre name="5a89" id="5a89" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--pre">const formatter = new Intl.NumberFormat('en-US', {<br>  style: 'currency',<br>  currency: 'USD',<br>  minimumFractionDigits: 2<br>})</pre>
           <pre name="b3ab" id="b3ab" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--pre">export default class App extends Component {<br> <br>  constructor(props) {<br>    super(props)<br>    this.state = {<br>      cosmic: this.props.cosmic,<br>      stats: {<br>        revenue: 'Loading...',<br>        users: 'Loading...',<br>        cancellations: 'Loading...'<br>      },<br>      users: [],<br>      fetchingRevenue: true,<br>      fetchingUsers: true,<br>    }<br>  }</pre>
           <pre name="fa83" id="fa83" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--pre">  fetchData() {<br>    this.getRevenue();this.getUsers();this.getCancellations()<br>  }</pre>
           <pre name="d06f" id="d06f" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--pre">  componentDidMount() {<br>    this.fetchData()<br>    setInterval(() =&gt; {<br>      this.fetchData()<br>    }, 60000)<br>  }</pre>
           <pre name="f762" id="f762" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--pre">  getRevenue(cosmic) {<br>    this.setState({ fetchingRevenue: true})<br>    async.series([<br>      callback =&gt; {<br>        Cosmic.getObject(this.state.cosmic, { slug: 'subscriptions' }, (err, response) =&gt; {<br>          callback(null, response.object)<br>        })<br>      },<br>      callback =&gt; {<br>        Cosmic.getObjectType(this.state.cosmic, { type_slug: 'users' }, (err, response) =&gt; {<br>          callback(null, response.objects.all)<br>        })<br>      }<br>    ], (err, results) =&gt; {<br>      let subscriptions = results[0], users = results[1];<br>      let currentStats = this.state.stats<br>      currentStats.revenue = formatter.format(users.map(user =&gt;<br>        parseInt(subscriptions.metadata[`${user.metadata.subscription_type}_price`].replace('$', ''))<br>      )<br>      .reduce((sum, val) =&gt; sum + val))<br>      this.setState({ stats: currentStats })<br>      this.setState({ fetchingRevenue: false })<br>    })<br>  }</pre>
           <pre name="7d51" id="7d51" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--pre">  getUsers(cosmic) {<br>    this.setState({ fetchingUsers: true })<br>    Cosmic.getObjectType(this.state.cosmic, { type_slug: 'users' }, (err, response) =&gt; {<br>      if (err) {<br>        currentStats = this.state.stats<br>        currentStats.users = 'Error'<br>        this.setState({ stats: currentStats })<br>      } else {<br>        let currentStats = this.state.stats<br>        currentStats.users = isNaN(response.total) ? 0 : response.total<br>        this.setState({ stats: currentStats })<br>        this.setState({ users: response.objects.all })<br>        this.setState({ fetchingUsers: false })<br>      }<br>    })<br>  }</pre>
           <pre name="1711" id="1711" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--pre">  getCancellations(cosmic) {<br>    this.setState({ fetchingCancellations: true})<br>    Cosmic.getObject(this.state.cosmic, { slug: 'subscriptions' }, (err, response) =&gt; {<br>      if (err) {<br>        currentStats = this.state.stats<br>        currentStats.users = 'Error'<br>        this.setState({ stats: currentStats })<br>      } else {<br>        let currentStats = this.state.stats<br>        currentStats.cancellations = isNaN(response.object.metadata.cancellations) ? 0: response.object.metadata.cancellations<br>        this.setState({ stats: currentStats })<br>        this.setState({ fetchingCancellations: false })<br>      }<br>    })<br>  }</pre>
           <pre name="0860" id="0860" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--pre">  render() {<br>    return (<br>      &lt;div className="container"&gt;<br>        &lt;Loader loadingState={this.state.fetchingUsers || this.state.fetchingRevenue || this.state.fetchingCancellations} /&gt;<br>        &lt;StatsContainer stats={this.state.stats} /&gt;<br>        &lt;UserList users={this.state.users}/&gt;<br>      &lt;/div&gt;<br>    )<br>  }<br>}</pre>
           <p name="282c" id="282c" class="graf graf--p graf-after--pre">We’re now left with four stateless functional components to build out. These are:</p>
           <p name="2612" id="2612" class="graf graf--p graf-after--p"><strong class="markup--strong markup--p-strong">1. Loader:</strong></p>
           <pre name="26c0" id="26c0" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--p">import ReactLoading from 'react-loading'</pre>
           <pre name="8c81" id="8c81" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--pre">const Loader = ({ loadingState }) =&gt;<br>  &lt;div className="row" style={{display: loadingState ? 'block' : 'none' }}&gt;<br>    &lt;div className="col-xs-12"&gt;<br>      &lt;div className="pull-right"&gt;<br>        &lt;ReactLoading height='20px' width='20px' type="spin" color="#444" /&gt;<br>      &lt;/div&gt;<br>    &lt;/div&gt;<br>  &lt;/div&gt;</pre>
           <pre name="674f" id="674f" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--pre">export default Loader</pre>
           <p name="f248" id="f248" class="graf graf--p graf-after--pre">Which makes use of the handy <code class="markup--code markup--p-code">react-loading</code> package.</p>
           <p name="f9f2" id="f9f2" class="graf graf--p graf-after--p"><strong class="markup--strong markup--p-strong">2. StatsContainer:</strong></p>
           <pre name="b68a" id="b68a" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--p">import StatTicker from './StatTicker'</pre>
           <pre name="b9d2" id="b9d2" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--pre">const StatsContainer = ({ stats }) =&gt;<br>  &lt;div className="row"&gt;{Object.keys(stats).map((key, index) =&gt;<br>      &lt;div key={index} className="col-md-4 text-center"&gt;&lt;StatTicker name={key} value={stats[key]} /&gt;&lt;/div&gt;<br>    )}<br>  &lt;/div&gt;<br><br></pre>
           <pre name="4b5b" id="4b5b" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--pre">export default StatsContainer</pre>
           <p name="49db" id="49db" class="graf graf--p graf-after--pre"><strong class="markup--strong markup--p-strong">3. StatTicker:</strong></p>
           <pre name="20e4" id="20e4" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--p">const StatTicker = ({ name, value }) =&gt;<br>  &lt;div&gt;&lt;h3 className="lead text-muted"&gt;{name}&lt;/h3&gt;&lt;h1 className="text-primary"&gt;{value}&lt;/h1&gt;&lt;/div&gt;</pre>
           <pre name="1646" id="1646" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--pre">export default StatTicker</pre>
           <p name="0f27" id="0f27" class="graf graf--p graf-after--pre">and finally…</p>
           <p name="a6e5" id="a6e5" class="graf graf--p graf-after--p"><strong class="markup--strong markup--p-strong">4. UserList:</strong></p>
           <pre name="39f8" id="39f8" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--p">const UserList = ({ users, deleteUser }) =&gt;<br>  &lt;div style={{marginTop: 50 + 'px'}} className="row"&gt;<br>    &lt;div className="col-xs-12"&gt;<br>      &lt;h4 className="pull-left lead"&gt;All Users:&lt;/h4&gt;<br>      &lt;table className="table table-responsive table-hover"&gt;<br>        &lt;thead&gt;<br>          &lt;tr&gt;<br>            &lt;th&gt;Stripe ID&lt;/th&gt;<br>            &lt;th&gt;First Name&lt;/th&gt;<br>            &lt;th&gt;Last Name&lt;/th&gt;<br>            &lt;th&gt;Email&lt;/th&gt;<br>          &lt;/tr&gt;<br>        &lt;/thead&gt;<br>        &lt;tbody&gt;<br>          {users.map((user, index) =&gt;<br>            &lt;tr key={index}&gt;<br>              &lt;td&gt;{user.metadata.stripe_id}&lt;/td&gt;<br>              &lt;td&gt;{user.metadata.first_name}&lt;/td&gt;<br>              &lt;td&gt;{user.metadata.last_name}&lt;/td&gt;<br>              &lt;td&gt;{user.metadata.email}&lt;/td&gt;<br>            &lt;/tr&gt;<br>          )}<br>        &lt;/tbody&gt;<br>      &lt;/table&gt;<br>    &lt;/div&gt;<br>  &lt;/div&gt;<br><br></pre>
           <pre name="2199" id="2199" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--pre">export default UserList</pre>
           <h3 name="108f" id="108f" class="graf graf--h3 graf-after--pre">Integrate Stripe&nbsp;Webhooks</h3>
           <p name="9987" id="9987" class="graf graf--p graf-after--h3">To get our cancelled subscriber count, we’ll udpate a <code class="markup--code markup--p-code">cancellations</code> metafield in our Cosmic <code class="markup--code markup--p-code">Subscriptions</code> object. To do this, we'll receive a webhook from Stripe through our Express app every time we delete a subscription on Stripe.</p>
           <ol class="postList">
            <li name="b035" id="b035" class="graf graf--li graf-after--p">Set up webhooks in Stripe and point them to the domain your Express app is deployed to.</li>
            <li name="a4e7" id="a4e7" class="graf graf--li graf-after--li">Create an <code class="markup--code markup--li-code">api</code> route at <code class="markup--code markup--li-code">CosmicUserBlog/routes/api.js</code> and <code class="markup--code markup--li-code">require</code> it in <code class="markup--code markup--li-code">App.js</code>.</li>
            <li name="c173" id="c173" class="graf graf--li graf-after--li">Handle POST requests with a <code class="markup--code markup--li-code">switch</code> statement acting on <code class="markup--code markup--li-code">req.body</code>. When Stripe sends us a subscription cancellation webhook, <code class="markup--code markup--li-code">req.body.type</code> will be <code class="markup--code markup--li-code">customer.subscription.deleted</code>.</li>
            <li name="b595" id="b595" class="graf graf--li graf-after--li">Delete the User object from Cosmic, get the Subscription object from Cosmic, shallow copy the object, increment <code class="markup--code markup--li-code">metadata.cancellations</code>, then use Cosmic's REST API to push the changes to the object.</li>
            <li name="12c6" id="12c6" class="graf graf--li graf-after--li">Respond with a <code class="markup--code markup--li-code">200</code> code so Stripe can confirm receipt of the webhook.</li>
           </ol>
           <p name="c43d" id="c43d" class="graf graf--p graf-after--li">Here’s the finshed product:</p>
           <pre name="ab03" id="ab03" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--p">var express = require('express')<br>var router = express.Router()<br>var cosmic = require('cosmicjs')<br>var axios = require('axios')</pre>
           <pre name="510d" id="510d" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--pre">router.post('/', function(req, res) {<br>  event = req.body<br>  switch (event.type) {<br>    case 'customer.subscription.deleted':<br>      cosmic.deleteObject(req.app.locals.config, { slug: 'user', write_key: req.app.locals.config.bucket.slug }, function (err, response) {<br>        cosmic.getObject(req.app.locals.config, { slug: 'subscriptions' }, function (err, response) {<br>          var currentObject = response.object<br>          currentObject.metadata.cancellations = currentObject.metadata.cancellations + 1<br>          currentObject.metafield.cancellations.value = currentObject.metadata.cancellations + 1<br>          currentObject.write_key = req.app.locals.config.bucket.write_key<br>          axios({<br>            method: 'put',<br>            url: `https://api.cosmicjs.com/v1/${req.app.locals.config.bucket.slug}/edit-object`,<br>            data: currentObject<br>          }).then(function (axRes) {<br>            console.log('Success')<br>          }).catch(function (axError) {<br>            console.log('Error')<br>          })<br>        })<br>      })<br>      return res.json({ received: true})<br>      break;<br>    default:<br>      return res.json({ received: false })<br>  }<br>});</pre>
           <pre name="2b3c" id="2b3c" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--pre">module.exports = router</pre>
           <h3 name="b392" id="b392" class="graf graf--h3 graf-after--pre">Deploy</h3>
           <p name="35df" id="35df" class="graf graf--p graf-after--h3">To tell Cosmic what your extension is, you’ll need to add <code class="markup--code markup--p-code">extension.json</code> to your <code class="markup--code markup--p-code">dist</code>folder. We'll configure our extension like this:</p>
           <pre name="f296" id="f296" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--p">// dist/extension.json</pre>
           <pre name="fa5c" id="fa5c" class="graf graf--pre graf-after--pre">{<br>  "title": "Subscription Management",<br>  "font_awesome_class": "fa-gears",<br>  "image_url": ""<br>}</pre>
           <h3 name="5a7c" id="5a7c" class="graf graf--h3 graf-after--pre">Conclusion</h3>
           <p name="5ae9" id="5ae9" class="graf graf--p graf-after--h3">Using Cosmic JS, Express, Stripe, and React, we’ve built both a monetizable blog that lets our readers subscribe to read premium content and a convenient dashboard to view data about our blog. We’ve integrated Stripe for secure payments and we’ve built an app that does as much as we want it to do with room to grow.</p>
           <p name="a8b8" id="a8b8" class="graf graf--p graf-after--p">With how quickly we’ve been able to build our app and with the simplicity of deploying and maintaining it, it’s clear that Cosmic JS is one of a kind in its API first approach to content management. Clearly, CosmisJS is a money maker.</p>

           <p name="c4e8" id="c4e8" class="graf graf--p graf-after--p graf--trailing"><em class="markup--em markup--p-em">Matt Cain builds smart web applications and writes about the tech used to build them.
